   yā gatistasya vipulā śāstravidyā ca vaidikī /	yA gatiH tasya vipulA SAstra vidyA ca vEdikI /
   karmaṇā cāpi miśreṇa kevalaṃ vidyayāpi vā // LiP_2,55.41 //	karmaNA ca api miSreNa kevalam vidyayA api vA // LiS _2,55.41 //
   nivṛttiścāsya viprasya bhavedbhaktiśca śāśvatī /	nivRttiH ca asya viprasya Bavet BaktiH ca SASvatI /
   mayi nārāyaṇe deve śraddhā cāstu mahātmanaḥ // LiP_2,55.42 //	mayi nArAyaNe deve SradDA ca astu mahAtmanaH // LiS _2,55.42 //
   vaṃśasya cākṣayā vidyā cāpramādaśca sarvataḥ /	vaMSasya ca akzayA vidyA ca apramAdaH ca sarvatas /
   ityājñā brahmaṇastasmāttasya sarvaṃ mahātmanaḥ // LiP_2,55.43 //	iti AjQA brahmaNaH tasmAt tasya sarvam mahAtmanaH // LiS _2,55.43 //
   ṛṣayaḥ procuḥ	RzayaH procuH
   ṛṣeḥ sūtasya cāsmākameteṣābhapi cāsya ca /	RzeH sUtasya ca asmAkam etezABapi ca asya ca /
   nāradasya ca yā siddhistīrthayātrāratasya ca // LiP_2,55.44 //	nAradasya ca yA sidDiH tIrTayAtrA ratasya ca // LiS _2,55.44 //
   prītiśca vipulā yasmā dasmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa // LiP_2,55.45 //	prItiH ca vipulA yasmE dasmAkam romaharzaNa // LiS _2,55.45 //
   sā sadāstu virūpākṣaprasādāttu samantataḥ /	sA sadA astu virUpAkza prasAdAt tu samantataH /
   evamukteṣu vipreṣu nārado bhagavānapi // LiP_2,55.46 //	evam uktezu viprezu nAradaH BagavAn api // LiS _2,55.46 //
   karābhyāṃ suśubhāgrābhyāṃ sūtaṃ pasparśivāṃstvaci /	karAByAm su SuBa agrAByAm sUtam pasparSivAn= tvaci /
   svastyastu sūta bhadraṃ te mahādeve vṛṣadhvaje // LiP_2,55.47 //	svasti astu sUta Badram te mahAdeve vRzaDvaje // LiS _2,55.47 //
   śraddhā tavāstu cāsmākaṃ namastasmai śivāya ca // LiP_2,55.48 //	SradDA tava astu ca asmAkam namaH tasmE SivAya ca // LiS _2,55.48 //
   iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge pañcapañcāśattamodhyāyaḥ	iti SrI liFga mahApurANe uttara BAge paQca paQcASat tamaH DyAyaH
   samāptaṃ caitallaiṅgottarārdham	samAptam cEtat lEFga uttara arDam
